These constructions can be explored in a very natural way by dragging, rotating and manipulating the geometric objects.\r\n\r\nThe constructions are saved locally or in the cloud. Embedding in interactive eBooks or HTML export is also possible.\r\n\r\nsketchometry is free to use and is developed at the Center for Mobile Learning with Digital Technology of the Bayreuth
